98 function resetSaveLabel() {

100 $("#confirmationMessage").removeClass("unsucessfully-alert");

101 $("#confirmationMessage").text("");

102 }

103 function saveSuccessful() {

104 resetSaveLabel();

105 $("#confirmationMessage").addClass("sucessfully-alert");

106 $("#confirmationMessage").text("Your request was sent. Thank you!");

107 $("#confirmationMessage").show();

108 $("#confirmationMessage").fadeIn("1000").delay(2000).fadeOut('1500').hide(0);

109 }

110 function saveUnsuccessful() {

111 resetSaveLabel();

112 $("#confirmationMessage").addClass("unsucessfully-alert");

113 $("#confirmationMessage").fadeIn("1000").delay(2000).fadeOut('1500').hide(0);

114 $("#confirmationMessage").text("Save operation not completed");

115 $("#confirmationMessage").show();

116 }

184 function querystring(key) {

185 var re = new RegExp('(?:\\?|&)' + key + '=(.*?)(?=&|$)', 'gi');

186 var r = [],

187 m;

188 while ((m = re.exec(document.location.search)) != null) r.push(m[1]);

189 return r;

190 }

191 if (querystring("isDownloadEnabled").length > 0) {

192 isDownloadEnabled = querystring("isDownloadEnabled").length > 0 && (querystring("isDownloadEnabled")[0].toLowerCase() == 'true') ? true : false;

193 }

194 if (querystring("isViewMoreDetailsBtn").length > 0) {

195 isViewMoreDetailsBtn = querystring("isViewMoreDetailsBtn").length > 0 && (querystring("isViewMoreDetailsBtn")[0].toLowerCase() == 'true') ? true : false;

196 }

197 if (querystring("DisplayHotspotsOnKiosks").length > 0) {

198 isHotspotBtn = querystring("DisplayHotspotsOnKiosks").length > 0 && (querystring("DisplayHotspotsOnKiosks")[0].toLowerCase() == 'true') ? true : false;

199 }

200 if (querystring("openLinkInModal").length > 0) {

201 openLinkInModal = querystring("openLinkInModal").length > 0 && (querystring("openLinkInModal")[0].toLowerCase() == 'true') ? true : false;

202 }

215 function checkScreenSize(){

216 var newWindowWidth = $(window).width();

217 if (newWindowWidth < 481) {

218 var activeSlide = $(document).find('.collapse.in');

219 activeSlide.removeClass('in');

220 $('#allPlans').slick({

221 slidesToShow: 1,

222 arrows: true,

223 infinite: false

224 });

225 $('#availablePlans').slick({

226 slidesToShow: 1,

227 arrows: true,

228 infinite: false

229 });

230 }else{

231 try {

232 $('#allPlans').slick('unslick');

233 $('#availablePlans').slick('unslick');

234 } catch (e) {

235 console.log('Unable to unslick! This is not an error, this is just a log.')

236 }

237 }

238

239 var check = false;

240

241 $('#allPlans').on('beforeChange', function (event, slick, currentSlide, nextSlide) {

242 var activeSlide = $(document).find('.slick-current.slick-active');

243 var Section = activeSlide.find('.panel-collapse.collapse')

244 if (Section.hasClass('in')) {

245 check = true;

246 } else {

247 check = false;

248 }

249 });

250

251 $('#allPlans').on('afterChange', function (event, slick, currentSlide) {

252 if (check) {

253 var activeSlide = $(document).find('.collapse.in');

254 activeSlide.removeClass('in');

255

256 var activeSlide = $(document).find('.slick-current.slick-active');

257 var Section = activeSlide.find('.panel-collapse.collapse');

258 Section.addClass('in');

259 }

260 });

261

262 $('#availablePlans').on('beforeChange', function (event, slick, currentSlide, nextSlide) {

263 var activeSlide = $(document).find('.slick-current.slick-active');

264 var Section = activeSlide.find('.panel-collapse.collapse')

265 if (Section.hasClass('in')) {

266 check = true;

267 } else {

268 check = false;

269 }

270 });

271

272 $('#availablePlans').on('afterChange', function (event, slick, currentSlide) {

273 if (check) {

274 var activeSlide = $(document).find('.collapse.in');

275 activeSlide.removeClass('in');

276

277 var activeSlide = $(document).find('.slick-current.slick-active');

278 var Section = activeSlide.find('.panel-collapse.collapse');

279 Section.addClass('in');

280 }

281 });

282 }

489 var ajaxCallStatus = {

490 Accepted: 1,

491 Error: 2

493 $('#requestForm').on('submit', function (e) {

494 e.preventDefault();

495 if ($('#requestForm').valid()) {

496 var formValues = $('form').serializeArray();

497 $('.btn.btn-primary').button('loading');

498 $('.validation-summary-errors').find('li').css('display', 'none');

499 $('.validation-summary-errors').addClass('validation-summary-valid').removeClass('validation-summary-errors');

500 var siteId = getParameterByName('siteID');

501 let lotids = sessionStorage.getItem(siteId);

502 if (lotids != null && lotids.trim() != "") {

503 for (var i = 0; i < formValues.length; i++) {

504 if (formValues[i].name == "Comments") {

505 formValues[i].value = formValues[i].value + "\nLotids: " + lotids;

506 }

507 }

508 }

509 var platformType = {};

510 platformType.name = 'Platform';

511 platformType.value = JSON.stringify(5);

512 formValues.push(platformType);

513 $.ajax({

514 url: '/Prospects/AddProspect',

515 type: 'post',

516 data: formValues,

517 success: function (data) {

518 if (typeof (data) != "undefined" && typeof (data.ajaxCallStatus) != "undefined" && data.ajaxCallStatus == ajaxCallStatus.Error) {

519 if ($('.zipCodeError').length == 0 && $('.validation-summary-valid ul').length > 0) {

520 $('.validation-summary-valid ul').append('<li class="zipCodeError">The Zip Code field is required.</li>');

521 $('.validation-summary-valid').addClass('validation-summary-errors').removeClass('validation-summary-valid');

522 }

523 else {

524 $('.validation-summary-valid ul').append('<li class="zipCodeError">The Zip Code field is required.</li>');

525 }

526 } else {

527 $('#myModal').modal('toggle');

528 document.getElementById('requestForm').reset();

529 showSuccessModel();

530 switch (requestInfoSource) {

531 case "Right": logGAEvent("Request-Info-right", "ISP", "form-submit_r");

532 break;

533 case "Bottom": logGAEvent("Request-Info-bottom", "ISP", "form-submit");

534 break;

535 case "Lot": logGAEvent("Request-Info-lot", "ISP", "form-submit_l");

536 break;

537 }

538 }

539 $('.btn.btn-primary').button('reset');

540 },

541 error: function (data) {

542 saveUnsuccessful();

543 $('.btn.btn-primary').button('reset');

544 }

545 })

546 }

547 });
